--- 帖子 #1 ---
I think its funny everyone is always speaking

of the Holy Grail. of trading "if I just get the right 10 tools"

the big boys know the tools don't really matter

You want to win?

They all say find a set up & use one tool as a trigger. ONE TOOL !!

But they also know the H.G. of trading is time frame trading

They never use more then 2 tools (any number of MAs count as 1 tool)

But they use 2- 3 or more time frames

& 1 or 2 tools on those time frames.

The tools really don't matter

see for yourself use your favour tool

or just try one of the following

a. Sars b. 5/6 Ema cross c.5/5 open/close Ema cross or any other MA set

d. Stoch what ever setting you like e. MACD

and put it on 3 time frames a. day b 4 hour c. 30 min (or hour)

and watch for all three to line up & you will win!! like 90-95%

take the day tool off & you will still win like 85-90% of the time

some tools are better then other & some are easier to work with.

But not by much

30 min chart

the Big blue line shows the trend from the day Stoch is up

the small blue line shows the trend from is 4 hour stoch is up

the Blue arrows are from the 30 min stoch below and show the trend is up

just try it for yourself -

the problem with this Idea is its hard to sell ebooks & make a lot of money!!!

--- 帖子 #10 ---
You are so right about this.  It is not the indicator or indicators you use but using the same indicator(s) on multiple time frames.  If they agree on multiple time frames the probability of success is extremely high.

I know this and I (theoretically) practice this, and it is every time that I violate my own rules that I get burned.

The only improvement that I would suggest is that you look at the relationship between the volatility of the pair and the time frames you select to apply to it.  In my experience, the more volatile the pair, the shorter the time frames I use successfully.  You might want to take a look at this some time.

I think this way of entry is really good. I also combine  entry/exit in relation to how close the MA21,62 or R/S/Pivot/Fib. retr. are at the moment of entry/exit. The mention points are also go for placing S/L.

--- 帖子 #39 ---
You can put more or less anything you want in the same indicator window just by dragging it from the navigator window into the indicator window you already have open.

If you are going to do this, then I suggest making each time frame stochastic  different colours.  You can do this in the colour window of the indicator.  You can set the timeframe on the stochastic in the input window of the indicator.

--- 帖子 #42 ---
I did a backtest on EURUSD from 1/25-today.

1. Just using the closing values of the bar after the stochs cross.

2. Only using the daily and 4hr stochs for trade initiation.

3. Close position when they cross back.

21 Total trades  17 wins/4 losses.   76% win ratio

Net pip gain including 2 pip spread.  718 pips

Largest Gain  - 101

Largest Loss  - 3

Not conclusive by any means just trying to be helpful.

Not bad for 8 weeks worth of work!

--- 帖子 #65 ---
Hi Guys,

just a heads up for an observation I made in your screenshots that **might** make it looking a little better than it actually is.

Please don`t take this as critisism. I just try to point out a source of a possible error which can be avoided.

Problem:

If you draw the line on the daily chart when a stoch cross gets confirmed, you have to draw the line on the new bar that just started building.

If you draw it on the bar thar that just closed, and you switch to the 30 min timeframe, the line on the 30 min chart will appear in the beginning of the day that confirmed the cross. Which is completely wrong and might lead to successfull backtesting when actually it is not.

Same for 4 hour lines.

GBP/JPY just confirmed crossed stochs on 4H. I took screens to illustrate what I mean

4H chart confirmed cross:

--- 帖子 #66 ---
And here how the same line draws on the 30m chart:

(the line should be at the 12:00 bar on the 30 min chart)

And if you use the MTF indicator to draw the lines, you obviously have todraw it t the end of the longer timeframe period, not where the actual cross happened on the MTF indicator.

--- 帖子 #103 ---
I don't do that - I do it by hand

I do one chart per pair

& move the time frames on it

I start with the day time frame

& draw a line where the stoch crosses (fat line)

then move to the 4 hour - (the day line is still on it)

I then place the thin line on the 4 hour chart where the stoch crosses

I then move to the 30 min - (the 2 lines are still on it)

& I have the 30 min stoch which I put the arrows from

the charts I use are MT4 & OANDA

& you can move the time frames & still keep the lines one

others do have programs you can get all three

but I have tried a few & they work

but I fould doing it by hand is still better

--- 帖子 #105 ---
Just a few thoughts of what I have found!

does anyone have their own wisdom they would like to add!Forex is great but you trade at your own risk! Not mine! Find a good honest broker that doesn’t bet against you-I use OANDA Candles work- I don’t think they should! I don’t know why they do - they just do!  The more tools you use the more you lose! One or two is lots-really! Multi-Time frames are the key to trading forex. The higher the time frame the easier it is to see the trend & so trade.  Use lower time frames as for buy & sell signs. Learn as much as you can from anywhere you can. KISS works best ( keep it simple smarty)  Follow the trend- till you can don’t trade!!! Follow your trading plan- till you can don’t trade!!! Learn to draw Trend lines - Support & Resistance & Channels- Its money in the bank. You will have loses – So have a stop loss always - I use 35 pip SL. Don't be the 1st one to the party- Don't be the last one to leave the party.  You don't have to get every "pip-pip" to have fun EUR/USD, USD/JPY, USD/CHF, EUR/JPY Are the easiest to trade and in that order  Price is a false mistress- momentum is a faithful wife!!

--- 帖子 #106 ---
I go out normal in stages

I normal go in 3 or 4 lots

1st lot 10 pips +spread & out

2nd lot 25 pips+ spread & out

3rd (4th) lot I move the sl up to 5 more then I buy in for

& I do as I like in the exit

1.by candles

2 the crossing of the 30 min stoch

3.the crossing of the 4 hour stoch- think this is likely the best

but if I don't like the way it looks- I will bail after 10 pips + spread

I did 3 times today more then I do normally - all 3 times I was right

The reason I think for today was so many of the pairs on the day stoch

were in the 20 or 80 % range - I never like when that is the case

you can have big moves opp the last trend very fast I have found

hope that helps

last-- the trend thing add a slow stoch at setting 14,3,3  & only trade with it

it will be right 85% its to slow to be a trigger but will save your bacon.

doing fibs & ems & stoch???? - stay with one

--- 帖子 #112 ---
Few words about channels, take for example Cable (GBPUSD). Recently it tends to "channelize" but fortunately it becomes normal again.

When you look at charts there are long vertical candles and quite long, ripped moves at about 45 degrees angle where normal elliot wave should be. Don't trade this. On Cable you can find channels in all timeframes, they hit them exactly to the point and reverse but also they can ignore it at all without a reason. I've had trades when market channelized and jumped even 30 points up and down to suddenly brake off in an unpredictable direction - stronger move up followed by a long candle down... In that case close and wait, it's so sick. Market can go 100 points this way in any direction, don't try to predict. Step back!!

Use channels only as TEB sugested as an exit point and never as a reversal.

Good luck

--- 帖子 #136 ---
Blanca,

Consider the Daily to show the long-term trend. The 4Hr will show an intermediate trend.. below about 1Hr consider it the short-term trend.

Analyze the charts a bit to see what you are comfortable with. If The daily shows Up and you are waiting for 4Hr & 30min confirmation, you are basically trading the long-term trend, but waiting for intermediate & short-term confirmation (being pickier with your entries).

If you ignore the daily trend & only use the 4hr & 30min, then you are trading the intermediate trend (of which there are quite a few per day) and using the 30min to pick your entry. There will be many such opportunities per day at this level.

Many traders advocate NOT trading against the longer-term trend (in this case either the daily or 4hr could be considered the longer-term trend). You may wish to consider using the daily with the more volatile pairs - that way you only trade in the direction of the long-term trend. Ultimately tho, which one you use is up to you and your own comfort level!

Hope this helps!

Daemien

--- 帖子 #147 ---
I completely agree about exiting, it is more of an art than a science. You either try to scalp a preset amount (e.g 20 pips) or you wait for it to tell you where its going.  There is another post:
http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...t=19391&page=9

they have an interesting concept using this method and a 25 wma with bands +/- 50 giving you a channel. Exit a long position when it hits the lower band, exit shorts when it hits the upper band. Not a bad concept, use a multiple set exit, take profit on half the position at say 15-20 and let the other half ride until it hits the opposing channel. That way you'll get the nice trends when they are available and make it out with some profit when they're not. We just have to play around with it to see what works best on what pair/time frame. Don't sweat the harshness, we're a learning community here and we need to be able to examine methods critically to obtain the greatest results and collectively figure out a way to get our stake of the forex pie.

Ron

--- 帖子 #235 ---
The Stochastic on the MTF indicator also includes RSI and CCI.  By adjusting the parameters, MTF indicators can be helpful screening tools; however, you are absolutely right, there is no substitute for actually studying the higher time frame charts.  You can see crossovers, angle and separation of the lines (strength of trend), trendlines etc.

The Higher Time Frames are the Bus Driver, the Lower Time Frames are the Passengers.

3. Never trade or be careful aroundAround economic news releases (in EST esp.7:00am 8:30am & 10:00 am 2:00pm) On fed day FOMC – take the afternoon off On Options Expiry day On triple Witching week 3rd Fri of March, June, Sept. Dec.- Trade only Monday & Tuesday Anytime volumes dries up – often 12:00-2pm EST The day before or after a holiday the 1st Thursday of every Quarter - Future contracts roll over Bank holidays where bond market is closed but not the stock market  The last trading day of the month – the day portfolio managers adjust there portfolios Any time you are not rested – or worried – or out of sorts – bad hair days Around the 100 points in the DOW ie 10,700 10,800 etc tends to make for a choppy market USA Fed Chairman speaks - take the afternoon off!!

Nice down leg so far this week with several entries along the way. For some reason this pair often seems to start it's movement (of the week?) in the Asian session which works quite well for me in my time zone (PST). I prefer methods of trading that tend to tell me when to be watching the market. If one knows when to "be there" then a lot of tedious screen watching can be avoided while still catching the most favourable moves for the week - that's right, I tend to think weekly pips rather than intraday. Just found that's the way it works best for me. Lets me even have a life .

4 hour chart

30 min Chart

you are in

--- 帖子 #497 ---
I need some clarification: The rules as I had them when I programmed the EA are not working; the system fails miserably under the following rules:

This is for using the Stoch(5,3,3) on Daily, 4-hour, and 30-min charts. Check the daily cycle: If the %K > %D and the %D has just crossed above 20, then we have a BULLISH daily signal. (Opposite for BEARISH).  Check the 4-hour cycle: Same signal rules as the daily but applied to the 4-hour Stoch.  If the Daily cycle is BULLISH and the 4-Hour cycle is BULLISH and...

If the %K > %D and the %D has just crossed above 20, for the 30-min Stoch, then we have a BUY signal; so GO LONG. (Opposite for short orders).

This was tested on EUR/USD dating back to 1999. Why does it fail? Well look at the attached chart. There is clearly an up trend yet the system keeps trying to sell, to go short. This is because look at the Daily stoch on the chart, it is in the OVERBOUGHT region, so it is giving BEARISH signals. The problem is that the stochastics (as well as most oscillators) have a tendancy to "stick" to the top side (overbought region) during an up trend and vice versa for a down trend.

Now I don't doubt that this general strategy of multiple time frames with one indicator works, in fact I like it a lot. But there must be some rules you are applying that I have not considered...maybe you are applying these rules subconsiously, but let's try and uncover them. For example: Maybe if the stoch is overbought and gives a bearish signal, but then later turns back around and crosses back above 80, then that should restore the bullish signal...

Any thoughts?

Thanks,

mathematician

--- 帖子 #546 ---
I did a course through a well know Canadian forex mentor that teaches multiple time frame (MTF) trading. Out of all the trading styles on FF MTF is what I have come back to, so I'm very happy to see this thread. Thanks.

On USD, Eur and Gbp - Yen I use 4 hour and 1 hour charts (recently changed from 30 min chart). I have standard MACD for divergence, 8 3 3 stoch, Williams % R on 14 and the Daily Fozzy thread's 8 sma, 8 rsi, Bol band combo on all time frames.

For other currencies that I watch (GBP, CHF and EUR - USD) I use 4hr, 1 hr and 30 min. I sometimes look at lower charts 15 and 5 min but thats more for scalping and I'm trying to move away from that.

OK I look for 2 time frames for stoch and W's % R to go overbought/sold. Once the higher time frame has gone OB/OS I look at the lower time frame for the daily fozzy indicator sma to cross the rsi and the final entry hurdle is for W's % R to cross the -50 line (which I have added to set alerts). This filter seems to help a great deal in keeping losing trades down.

Other things like macd or stoch divergence, candles, chart patterns, fib levels etc etc help of course but the above confluence of events works for me and I suppose thats what its all about.

Perhaps you say I am over using indicators you are probably right!! Anyway hope this might help tweak the basics of a successful trading style.

--- 帖子 #553 ---
Tebe,  It's  the  same  system as  your  method

I  have  just attempted  to  refine it a  little .....

I use
1 hr  bar for  larger  time  frame

and  15 min bars  for smaller  time frame

------------------------------------------

and  use

the touch  of Lower Bollinger Bands
instead  of  looking  for  cross of  Stochastics

-----------------------------------------------

There are  too  many  Stochastic  cross overs -

and  most  lag  behind  price , so  I find that  looking  for  the

touch  of  a  lower  Bolliner Bands ( if bullish ) to be more  reliable

than looking for  Stochatics or MACD  to  cross  over  .

---------------------------------------------------------

So here's how  it goes ( Bullish Senario )

Step1 - get a 1 hr  bar chart and apply Bollinger  Bands (21 bar Setting )

Step2 - make  sure price is  touching Lower Bands  on 1 hr bar chart

Step3 - after you know  that price  is  touching Lower Bollinger Bands  on

............on 1 hr  chart ,  then open  a  15 min chart

Step4 -  draw  your  1st Paralell Line on the  15 min chart and  label it 1 hr

Step5-  on the 15 min bar chart -watch  and  wait  for price to  rally and  pull  back

............. and  touch  the  Lower  Bollinger  Lines , and use as potential entry signal .

Step6- Only buy if  price  is touching Lower Bollinger Lines on 15 min charts !

It's That Simple !.................  Just as  you already say .

--- 帖子 #599 ---
Mathematician

I hope you complete the EA - I would like to use it to send/make alerts so that one does not have to watch all the charts all the time.

I have just finished reading the whole thread. I suggest the following rules to get started.

My understanding is that where the Stoch are relative to the 20 and 80 lines are where the discretionary part of the system comes in. I suggest therefore that you leave it out of the EA for now. I would also suggest to leave the rules around the 50 EMA out for now - they are (in my opinion) filters of the core system.

The core system as I understand it is:

Go long when:

On D1 chart %K>%D, and

On 4H chart %K>%D, and

On 30 min chart %K>%D

The opposite is used for shorts

If we have an EA - or maybe an indicator with alerts that notifies us when the above conditions are true then we may not miss it when it happens.

If you want to include the rules around the 20 and 80 lines I think they should be ignored on the D1 chart. From how I understand the position of the Stoch relative to the 20 and 80 lines are most important on the 4 hour chart.

Teb - please confirm that the rules above is correct

--- 帖子 #609 ---
---------------------------------------------------------------

Ok, here it is ........ ( See  Chart Below )

I use
1 hr  bar for  larger  time  frame

and  15 min bars  for smaller  time frame

------------------------------------------

and  use

the touch  of Lower Bollinger Bands
instead  of  looking  for  cross of  Stochastics

-----------------------------------------------

There are  too  many  Stochastic  cross overs -

and  most  lag  behind  price , so  I find that  looking  for  the

touch  of  a  lower  Bolliner Bands ( if bullish ) to be more  reliable

than looking for  Stochatics or MACD  to  cross  over  .

---------------------------------------------------------

So here's how  it goes ( Bullish Senario )

Step1 - get a 1 hr  bar chart and apply Bollinger  Bands (21 bar Setting )

Step2 - make  sure price is  touching Lower Bands  on 1 hr bar chart

Step3 - after you know  that price  is  touching Lower Bollinger Bands  on

............on 1 hr  chart ,  then open  a  15 min chart

Step4 -  draw  your  1st Paralell Line on the  15 min chart and  label it 1 hr

Step5-  on the 15 min bar chart -watch  and  wait  for price to  rally and  pull  back

............. and  touch  the  Lower  Bollinger  Lines , and use as potential entry signal .

Step6- Only buy if  price  is touching Lower Bollinger Lines on 15 min charts !

It's That Simple !.................  Just as  you already say .

--- 帖子 #616 ---
Read this again ! -  It  explains

---------------------------------------------------------

So here's how it goes ( Bullish Senario )

Step1 - get a 1 hr bar chart and apply Bollinger Bands (21 bar Setting )

Step2 - make sure price is touching Lower Bands on 1 hr bar chart

Step3 - after you know that price is touching Lower Bollinger Bands on

............on 1 hr chart , then open a 15 min chart

Step4 - draw your 1st Paralell Line on the 15 min chart and label it 1 hr Bar

--------( this is  the  1st thick brown line that  you see on the  charts )

Step5- on the 15 min bar chart -watch and wait for price to rally and pull back

............. and touch the Lower Bollinger Lines , and use as potential entry signal .

Step6- Only buy if price is touching Lower Bollinger Lines on 15 min charts !

------------------------------------------------------------------------

--- 帖子 #645 ---
Hi,

I've modified DigiStoch to serve us (hopefully) better than the original. It's simpler, much more adjustable and shows "our" stoch settings (default 553, Low/High, simple) but most of it, doesn't clutter the chart. Keep it simple!

This a preliminary release so please comment. I can add another stoch settings if required , maybe a sound alarm for custom TFs? I'm not an MQ4 master but it's not that hard

MidLevel defines where you consider signal to be weak. So if stoch is uptrend and over given number it changes to the darkest color, so you'll know how far it is to reversal zone. Set this for uptrend only.

--- 帖子 #646 ---
You cant use this and digistochs together, and will interfere regardless if they are on the chart or not. You should change all your object references to entirely different values than what is in digistochs.

--- 帖子 #647 ---
Hi Teb63,

I am following your thread and like your methods. There were also some interesting indicators.

At the same time I was busy with one which I think had more to do with your method.

It is still a bit under construction and I have a normal day job, so I cannot respond to many questions about my indicator.

One thing is for sure, you earn all the credit!

It uses vertical lines the same way you do.

You can handle 4 periods, but I have got them default on the 3 you mention. The lowest TF has the thinest line, the highest the thickest.

For each period/TF you can show more than 1 line, if you want. Default 1, except period 2, it is zero, because it is the default 1 hour period, which you don't use.

You can also change the MA method and pricefield.

If you think the line should shift 1 or more bars, you can change that.

For each period you can set an alert and/or a send mail.

Enjoy!

I don't know how you guys are putting real money on this stoch indicator, you guys need to understand the idea of this strategy, the indicators always tell you what happened before, they will never tell you what will happen in the future, and this strategy of 3 time frames tells you, your position at this time, I don't think an stoch is needed for this, better yet stoch is misleading meaning it will cross and uncross, which therefore trick you and clouds you from success. Forexpert310,

No offense , but do you trade...I mean for a living??

EURUSD opened @ 1.3366, above the daily Pivot which means the base is Long, this is confirmed with the daily Stochs and my own EMA’s.

It moved down below today's pivot at 1.3359 on a narrow daily range.

It just finished a Triangle Pattern and the downward movement is continuing

This sounds a lot like the newsletters I received when I started trading… you subscribe to every news letter and signal service (free) that you can find, hoping they will tell you something and after reading them when they arrive in your mailbox, and you sit back for a smoke you think to yourself…. I only watch the Stochs, enter in the direction of the daily trend followed by the 4hr and then 30 min, I may confirm an exit with the ema’s on larger TF.

Currently we are still in that same vicinity, and 2 scenarios are presenting it self Daily stochs is still up and not over bought, Daily ema’s is still upBut the 4hr stochs is down, and ema’s seem to be dropping like a sack of weed, as soon as they cross and the 30 min’s give me a good entry, I’ll scalp a quick 5-10 pips on the short.  4hr Stochs is down and the ema’s are turningKeep an eye on the Daily, as soon as they change and the ema’s is making a turn, wait for the 30 min, which will probable be in Oversold to give a good entry and away ya go for short.  Either way be patient and the money will come.

--- 帖子 #813 ---
Just finished reading the whole thread, unfortunatelly i seem to be late for the party you guys were having here, but anyways, i'll stick my 2 cents in here

First, i would like to address this guy:

forexexpert310 said:

What seems to be a ranging market on daily chart, will look like trending market on 30 min charts, agreed? Thus, from what you're saying, there's 80% ranging in forex, meaning 80% trending on 30min charts off which we make our entry here, am i correct? My point is that the point is to get the timeframes synchronized and you won't have a problem with ranging/tranding, sounding like such a great expert, i'm surprised you didn't realise that.

Secondly, you just said you're working on a system based on mathematics and statistics. Here's where i'm going to critisize you, if i may. I've taken many math courses and stats courses in the past years, first thing that i was thinking about stats: "i'm going to create a statistical model to predict future directions", guess what, no matter how good those models were, no matter how accurate the Rsqr i was getting and how small the errors were, i found out that it worked just like any other system - sometimes accurate, sometimes it would screw you up. What was the reason? It's the same one for which you're critisizing the stochs indicator - models were using the past data, thus they were telling me what had happened, not what will happen.

Now, how is the stochs calculated, do you know? Same thing my friend, the numbers are coming from past observations, so you can call this indicator a statistical/mathematical tool as well in principle.

What am i trying to say... I'm trying to say that it's normal to use the past to predict the future, this is what the stats is all about, this is the whole point of technical analysis.

Therefore, by critisizing this system, you frist of all, are critisizing your efforts.

Anyways, sorry If i sounded mean, i am only trying to present a counterargument to what you're saying. By the way, how are you going to implement a market psychology into your mathematical tools, any insite on that? Thnx

Now, sorry for a large post, but i'm not finished yet

Thank you TEB for sharing your method, i'm sure its simplisity has has helped a lot of guys here to see the importance of having several tf's in sync before taking a trade.

I've also noticed that some of the guys are not sure how the 50ema is used, what is "way above/below" the 50ema, how large a pip distance? Just an idea here: try adding 50CCI and add 200/-200 and 0 levels to it, and see how it works relative to the 50ema and price distance. cci is looking at the separation from the 50ema (or separation from the zero line), so if you have the cci above 200 line for instance, you know that it's in overbought and about to start turning. However, on its own, cci is useles, but I looked how it works in combination with all the stochs, it does a bit better job of describing the picture with regards price/50ema separation.

Also some good moves are missed when waiting for the price to be on the wrong side of the ema, sometimes it will not go into the wrong side but just bounce off it, so look at where the cci line is at the moment: i've found out, that once it's crossed the zero line, in 90% of the cases it'll keep going to the extreme level (the 200 level), and once it's crossed back from the extreme level, it'll come back to the zero line.

For cable i would suggest to use 250 levels, for euro 200 is enough imho.

If you don't find it helpful, then disregard this idea, 50ema will still do the trick, just need more eye training.

Once again, thnx for sharing yur system TEB.

Happy Easter all.

Hi guys

I am reading other threads & rereading mine to see who people are

& my emails ...and I see one question a number of times.

why do I not use the 5 min or the 15 min stoch

I did some tests before & to my surprise the 30 min stoch beats the 15 min stoch

well over 50 % but if you take out the false starts it wins in pips by quite a bit

that is of coarse comparing using just the 30 min stoch to using both the 15 min & 30 min stoch

if you use just the 15min stoch without the 30 min stoch you will get in faster

then with just the 30 min stoch but you get a lot more false reads.

you win more by using just one rather then using both always

in fact this is true every time you move up a time frame-

so the hour stoch beats the 30 mins etc...

if you want to make more pips -less trades -more boring

this makes sence as we are taking a bigger trend

I was borded today so I was playing with a pair I almost never trade

& have not for a few months so I don't have a feel for it

I tried a tests on the last few days

1st place I came to

the 30 min stoch beats the 15 min stoch

on the 2 trades I would have taken

see above two charts

Red arrow 30min stoch

Blue arrow 15 min stoch.

I might use the 5 min stoch with the 5 min

the reason I wouldn't use 15 & 30 stoch is because it is not tellme anything new

is because they are too close.

Its the same wave & same group of traders

I have said before its not price that is my main concern

Its movition of the pair.

the reason this is important is because on the higher TF have the big money

and they take days or weeks to change direction.

because they can not let price fall fast as they would lose to much money;

they would be betting against themselve

this fact is why the princible & the practies of stoch are a bit differant.

and why the hight the TF the better the rate of win-

because you move into the banks & the funds - the big boys

this is opp. to princible but really life.

& that is why I start with the day & work down

--- 帖子 #900 ---
I really like the idea of trading the trend... but always knew momentum shouldn't be completely ignored.   Trading the trend of the momentum is brilliant, no?

I also used various timeframes to trade... but always sepearte charts for each timeframe... then flipping through each chart.  "Combining" them onto one chart is another "Guiness moment" (BRILLIANT!) for me.

I couldn't sleep Thursday night and ended up reprogramming my system to take advantage of what I've learned on this thread.

Setup the Stoch's... setup daily timeframe, marked the cross and noted the trend (UP/DOWN), then changed timeframe to 4HR and looked for confirming cross.  If I got the confirming cross I marked it (also noting the trend matched the day) and adjusted the chart to read 30MIN to wait for the next cross that matched the trend direction.

THAT WORK SO WELL IT SCARED ME.

Now... the challenge came with the exits.  I felt using the 30MIN cross was a great entry... but could whipsaw my exit.  One I place the buy/sell I just backed it to the 4hr to wait for the cross to reverse.

Yeah... that cost me a  150pip profit plus another 100 to boot.

HOWEVER, upon licking my wounds after the market closed I noticed that if I had only used the 2 hour to take my exit cues from I would've protected the vast majority of my profit.

There are two things I've adjusted to TEB's system... using the 2 hour timframe for exit signal and I'm not worrying about the ema (though I do have it plotted).

Still, I'm new as a trader so I'm looking for any opinions on these variations.

BTW... VERY GRATEFUL for this thread and system TEB63... it's been helping me pop all sorts of little lightbulbs on.

Yep... I don't worry about the actual momentum, per se... just the TREND the momentum has.  If the day lines up with the 4 hr the trend is confirmed (assuming I'm understand TEB correctly).  Once the confirmation is there, it's a matter of entry and exit points... that's where the 30MIN tf comes in.  I like the idea of phasing out of a winning trade (TEB's suggestion) and plan on playing a bit with that idea as well (would've made some pips on Friday)!

I think to understand something you have to be able to know it well enough to teach it to someone else.  I'm sort of deconstructing TEB's first post in this thread... (to paraphrase)

1.  Keep it simple.

2.  Trade the trend.

3.  Use timeframes.

I see what people are doing with the system now, then I take that "finished product" and pull it apart and scatter the pieces around so I can "rebuild it."  By doing this not only do I have a working system, but one that I can actually understand the reason why it works.

I have to say... I don't think TEB's idea is rocket-science... that's why I grateful to TEB for sharing it.  Too often I've been looking for the complicated answer because if it looks complicated then it must work, right?

Simplicity is the most complicated thing there is... it's the hardest to see.

TEB isn't the first person to point out the obvious to me... just the first person I've actually HEARD!

Right place at the right time I guess... thanks again TEB!

--- 帖子 #912 ---
Here's how I trade this method:

Assume the 1D Stochs crosses up. I don't look at the levels where it happens (don't care if it happens under 20 or 50 or 80 or above 80).

Then look at the 4h - where does the up cross happen?

If it happens under 50 I will give full throttle, my whole percentage of risk which is between 1 and 3 % of my balance.

If it happens above 50 I only risk the half of my risk percentage which is 0.5 to 1.5 % of balance.

If the up cross establishes above 80 - I don't trade long !

Then look at 30min.

If up cross happens under 50 it is a long trade, if above 50 it is not a trade. I wait.

Exit:

I wait the 4h stochs to cross in the opposite direction.

The exit is the only thing I am not satisfied yet. But working on it....

Greetings from Greece

Freewheelin

--- 帖子 #941 ---
4X is hard!!

Okay

1.The simplist is just wait until the 3 stoch are all going in the same way

2. pip room . this is where it ges a little tricky

you can have all 3 stochs going the right way but be in a chop in other words flat market ..no trend no direction so as a filter do handle this I use 50EMA (& 20SMA) I want them no be on the wrong side of price .. this is so the trend has some where to go.

If you just use the 50EMA you will have fewer trade but will win almost alway! the 20SMA is the middle of the B. Band & is a great second piproom meter for strong trends & flater markets .. but not as good or faithful as the 50EMA and you do not have as much piproom with it ... & you don't need to use it .

that is really all you need to know about getting in.

I had only 4 trades yesterday for 10,15,25,37pips that was all I got

it was just an okay day .. Weds. thurs & friday where great days

--- 帖子 #982 ---
There seems to be some misunderstanding here. The indicator listed in the above thread is simply a noise maker for the stochastic cross in the particular timeframe window to which it is attached. It is not an indicator that "reads" a line up of stochastics for all three time frames.

--- 帖子 #983 ---
Again the confusion seems to be that this is an indicator that shows entries for this method. It is not! It is simply a noise maker for a stochastic cross in the particular timeframe being viewed. Hope that clears up the confusion.

--- 帖子 #1001 ---
Teb,

I looked at the charts and came to the conclusion that the 15,5,5 is not optimal for taking signals off of. However, what it does do is give assurance to the 5,3,3 signal/trigger. Look what happens when both are low at the 20 and crossing up together as opposed to the 15,5,5 not moving with the 5,3,3. It kind of lets you know if the move is going to be small or HUGE!

Also, I looked at it on the 1hr as you suggested by Mark Mcrae. It seems that if we get a set up according to your system, then check the 15,5,5 on the 1 hour and it agrees.... It's a strong probability.

Lastly, I looked at using the 15,5,5 as an exit on the 30 min chart and it seems to work well. Keeps you in a trade longer for more pips and avoids the 30 min 5,3,3 whipsaw that tends to happen.

Check out those 2 strategies on your charts and let me know what you think. As I said, the 15,5,5 has helped me alot!

Bago

--- 帖子 #1037 ---
Hello TEB... and All...

Lets see if I got it...

I don't want to bather you TEB with this... you explained this many times already... so I will put it the way I understand it... and... please someone who is already good at it, tell me if I I am doing it right...

***  "drawing of the lines" on the chart... *** say we start with D1 and are marking TOPS...

- one chart, D1 view...

[1] place line#1, at the 1st Stoch-crossing above 80 [counting from the right]... line-up line#1 with the highest near-by candle... there may be several mid-waves before the TOP Stoch from above 80 will reach the BOTTOM [below 20 reversal-point, which may be marked with line#1a]... all the smaller TF waves are happening between 1&1a...

- the same chart, H4 view [line#1 is already there]...

[2] place line#2, at the 1st Stoch-crossing above 80 [counting from the right]...  line-up line#2 with the highest near-by candle... there may be several mid-waves before the TOP Stoch from above 80 will reach the BOTTOM [below 20 reversal-point, which may be marked with line#2a]... all the smaller TF waves are happening between 2&2a...

- the same chart, H1 view [line#1,#2 are already there]...

[3] place line#3, at the 1st Stoch-crossing above 80 [counting from the right]...  line-up line#3 with the highest near-by candle... there may be several mid-waves before the TOP Stoch from above 80 will reach the BOTTOM [below 20 reversal-point, which may be marked with line#3a]... all the smaller TF waves are happening between 3&3a...

- the same chart, M15 view [line#1,#2,#3 are already there]......

[4] place line#4, at the 1st Stoch-crossing above 80 [counting from the right]...  line-up line#4 with the highest near-by candle... there may be several mid-waves before the TOP Stoch from above 80 will reach the BOTTOM [below 20 reversal-point, which may be marked with line#4a]... all the smaller TF waves are happening between 4&4a...

the idea is to see where, each TF's Stochs are positioned during their travel between +80 and -20... H4 is starting a new trend... M5.M15,M30,H1 will follow... enter/exit/magnification on Stochs crossing 80% or 20% from the outside, towards the middle 50%...

I am still not sure though if I understand TEB's system correctly...

BTW: Sma20 is almost same as Ema25... they also represent "0" line of MACD...

--- 帖子 #1048 ---
The Basics of the TEB SYSTEM

Most systems are mainly about price,

I think MTFT & esp. the stochs are better used

predicting monentun "the big Mo" then stating price.

there is my thinking

ie. I live very close to two of the bussies highways in N.A.

I can tell the direction & spead of the cars just by looking ..easy

(this is what most tools do well esp. on one time frame.)

but  as I look at the highway

I can also predict the spead & direction of the cars coming after.....why?

Because to change direction or spead of the cars

one of two things would have to happen.

1. A slow down or spead up must happen slowly.

why? because other wise you will have a crash

2. which is the other thing that can happen .. a crash

but both the Highways & the 4X are basical run by admin guys & computer

both of which do not like crashes... so both the HWs & 4X are very predictable

...with times of panic when the unpredicable happen... crashs

now the good news is in the 4x we have times ..call news & interst rate info.

that reset the whole thing & we start again

... these in fact take a lot of the crashs out of the 4X

you can for sure make money using MTFT & stochs to show price for sure

or make a lot more money using them to show you the big "mo"

& the big money.

TEB

--- 帖子 #1129 ---
Hey FX Surfer

How you doin? As far as me and the trend, I'm just doing the TEB thing. Actually, I'm sort of new to trend trading. I know that sounds funny in FX, but mostly what I've been doing is trading off support and resistance. You know, playing extended ranges for bounces, Fib retracements, etc. Those were part of my trades this week. I'm comfortable trading like that and have been successful, but I get tired of watching a pair move 100 pips to get to my entry spot. Also, sometimes you wait pretty long for a proper set up. I decided to find a way to get some of the big move, so here I am, and so far, so good.

To identify the trend, I just 'follow the book' according to TEB, that is, look for the daily and 4 hour stochs to agree, then get in when the 30 minute crosses. The only other thing so far is on a day when no daily and 4 hours agree, I dial it down to 4 hour, 1 hour, and 15 minute and do a little scalping. Using the 50 ema helps a lot.

I'm still missing quite a few trades but I'm still getting more comfortable all the time. I only got one trade today (woke up late!) and got 13 pips on the G/U.

I also like to trade the news. I know most people tell you not to, but it can be done successfully. It takes a lot of preparation and a good broker. If you like playing video games, you'll be good at news trading.

Anyway, long answer but I'm just doing it as written. By the way, 10 for 10 isn't normal for me, or at least it hasn't been. I've lost 10 in a row before. I hope those days are gone!

Richard

--- 帖子 #1153 ---
Hi traders,

I have improved my older version with the following:

Alert improvement:

Choose how many Time frames must be in line to give an alert (1,2,3 or 4).

Example:

period1                      = 30

period2                      = 60

period3                      = 240

period4                      = 1440
MaxNumberOfLinesP1    =    2

MaxNumberOfLinesP2    =    0

MaxNumberOfLinesP3    =    2

MaxNumberOfLinesP4    =    2

This means that the second time frame (= 1hr) is not being used (-> MaxNumberOfLinesP2 = 0)

The other time frames will allways show 2 lines in the LOWEST time frame (MaxNumberOfLinesP1 = 2, etc.).

If, during a new bar, the stochs cross over, there will be a pending line, until close. This pending line will always count as one of the lines. So if you have set 2 lines, the pending line will always be the first of the 2 lines.

In the above example you have chosen for 3 time frames with 2 lines maximum. If you click on a higher TF, the lines of the lowest will disappear.

Now you can choose when to show an alert:
AlertNrOfTFs = 3

1, 2 or 3 (3 is maximum in this case, because you only use 3 time frames).

Then there is an extra filter:

You can choose to handle different combinations:

(See complete set of parameters in Indicator)
Here you see time frame setups (if 3 TF's) for different cross overs:

extern string  Up_2Dn_3Up           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade" or empty string

extern string  Up_2Up_3Dn           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade"

extern string  Up_2Dn_4Up           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade"

extern string  Up_2Up_4Dn           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade"

extern string  Up_3Dn_4Up           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade"

extern string  Up_3Up_4Dn           = "Buy";     // "Buy"  or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_2Up_3Dn           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_2Dn_3Up           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_2Up_4Dn           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_2Dn_4Up           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_3Up_4Dn           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

extern string  Dn_3Dn_4Up           = "Sell";    // "Sell" or "NoTrade"

Here you can determine if you want to use the setups for an alert.

Let's look at the last one: "Dn_3Dn_4Up" = "Sell"

This could be a "sell" setup. The first TF is down, the second TF is not used, the third TF is down and the fourth TF is up.

If you don't want an alert for this setup, you just remove the "Sell" string.

Regards,

fewhills

--- 帖子 #1158 ---
Hi TEB,

Think you may have put the hourly blue line in the wrong place on the 5m chart example above.

You have the blue line on the hourly signal candle i.e 00.00 open and 01.00 close.

But on the 5m chart it is still showing on the 00.00 candle which is 00.00 open and 00.05 close, 55 minutes before the direction is given on the end of the hourly candle.

Hope this makes sense.

In this example if you wait for the hourly candle to close the 5m blue line needs to be on the 00.55-01.00 candle.

--- 帖子 #1162 ---
I this what happens is that when you draw a line is goes on the, for example candle that opens at 2pm.

Then when you change timeframes it stays on that 2pm open candle, so

On the 1 hour chart it will be on the 2pm open - 3pm close candle

On the 30m chart it will be on the 2pm open - 2.30 close candle

On the 5 min chanrt it will be on the 2pm open - 2.05 close candle.

etc etc

On the 1 min chart it will be on the 2pm open - 2.01 close candle.

--- 帖子 #1163 ---
but is that not what I want to happen?

TEB

--- 帖子 #1164 ---
Depends on if you wait for the hourly candle to close before starting to look for entries.

If the trigger is given on the 2pm-3pm hourly candle and you wait for it to close as complete confirmation, when you drop down to the 5m chart the line needs to be on the 2.55-3.00 candle.

The result is truly AMAZING!!! test it out and see for urself guys!!

--- 帖子 #1222 ---
Hi,

One of the members requested a version for TEB2.

I made the crossover[4]. The default settings can be used for TEB2.

2 x 1hr stoch (5,3,3) and (14,3,3)

and

2 x 5 min stoch (5,3,3) and (14,3,3)

Each stoch now can have it's own settings and own colors. You can play with them and fit them as you like.

Of course you can use this one for TEB1 system too. Just change parameters, like in crossover[3].

Forgot to say: only stoch cross overs are detected! I will have a look at %stoch cross overs and make this in the next version.

Regards,

fewhills

Hi Bagovino,

I dont want to post here how i trade with the Stoch, TEB63 spend a bunch of hour to help you all in this thread. Follow what it do with TEB2 system. MultiTimeframe is the way to go but anybody who follow this thread already know that anyway.The main reason why i posted here is because i see TEB63 going in many direction trying to find the perfect system and i wanted to tell him he already have one right here.

When i started to trade i was lost in so many system, and at the end (9 month later) i was trading sucessfully the first one hehe.Its easy to get lost in forex like any other market.Bank trader learn to manage money nothing more nothing less , at the university they didnt tell us how to trade lol if they was able to do that , every trader will take the same signal at the same time  .Its why its so important to stick with a system and trying to improve it for the rest of your life.The only indicator i use is a Stoch, dont need others. Some friend of me trade with a CCI, others trade with Macd, everybody is successfull. The reason why its important to not mix too much indicator its if you get 10 signal but 9 of them was in conflict with other indicator and you only took the last signal who was in agreement with all your indicator and your wrong, you maybe only lost 10-20 pips but if you took all the 10 signal and 7-10 was a good one, you make maybe 120 pips, and you lost maybe 35 pips at the end of the day , so 95 pips in profit for one paire.

Lost is inevitable, cut it short and you will be fine and your wallet will grow like hell.Money management is the key , even with a 30/70 win ration if you get 7 lost of 15 pips but 3 win of 40 pips , you make money , not alot but its just a exemple of a realy crappy system with market order but you manage your lost and you let the winner run, not the bad one. Gain confidence in your system, you will not be scared to take a trade even if its a loosing one cuz you know your winner will be by far greater than your lossers.

Everybody can trade successfully in forex even if they cant move the market like bank can do.They just need to dont get lost at trying to find the perfect system who do no lost at all and start trading with a good one and stick with it. I explained why the market can move in one direction for no reason, so for the same reason a system cant be right every time.Its why its so important to spend hour and hour and hour to learn how to use your indicator and understand how it react with different type of market.

I hope you all a wonderfull trading day.

Best Regards,

EricFX

"Iceberg Formation" mean, when a bank want to sell by exemple 600M of euro , they will try to hide the ammount of money by placing alot of little order, so other bank will not bid against them cuz they didnt know they try to sell a bunch of money.That move the market realy fast in one direction when that happen.

EricFX

--- 帖子 #1291 ---
Hi,

I got alot of request for my Words document when it will be ready, so i decided to not make it and to put all the information directly on this thread. the only thing ill ask its to not ask any question if you didnt read the entire thread, i dont have alot of time to answer alot of question.

The Setup is :

SMI (Stochastic Momentum Index) 5/3/3/3, you can use a Full Stoch if you dont have this indicator.

Stochastic Slow, 14/3/3

TimeFrame : 30M/4H

PART 1:

Usualy i trade 10 paire but for all my exemple ill use EUR/USD, in the screenshot you see all trade i took from the 26 april until now on the 4H timeframe, the 3 Diamond is all trade i didnt took but all 3 was a good trade and the square was not a good one. the First diamond have a wierd shape, when you see a shape like that usualy the trend begin to loose it momentum, but in this one he didnt do that. The Second Diamond was too low for me to go short. For the last Diamond if you look at the momentum before it moved up, its was realy realy weak, so for me usualy ill wait for the Stock to go in the 70~ before taking a trade to see a better momentum. For the square, the stoch didnt reach near 25 so for me its a no trade to go long, too weak momentum to have a strong feeling in it.

For right now i just wanted to show the 4H chart cuz its your primary tool to trade,it show you where the price go and you get a better feeling of the momentum.If you just started to trade with the Stochastic , only trade this timeframe until you have a good confidence in the Stochastic, the Slow Stoch is your trigger, the SMI is your warning, the 80/20 line are your last entry , after that, too late if it was upper than 80 and lower 20 (i dont enter after it broke it by more than 5-6 point, if im in, good, if not , ill wait for the second signal)

The first 3 trade was in a sideway market, going up and down and we got 1 wispaw (The Square), Its why you need spend hour and hour and hour at looking at how react the Stoch in all type of market cuz its easy to follow a hard trend but in weak market you need to understand how it react. For all people who read that and think they only need to sell/buy when the Stoch cross and its done, good , that will make more money in my account, for the rest of you who will take time to study this indicator and learn how the market react with it, im sure you will be happy.

Ill post at the end of each day all signal we got with the Stoch on eur/usd ,and analise with you all how i read it, there alot of thing to learn from that indicator but i didnt have the time right now to write all thing i want to say in one post.But ill take the time after each day.

The last thing, if on the 4H the Stoch look wierd, dont try to see on the 30M if it look better, maybe it will look better but that will not make you a better market to trade

--- 帖子 #1298 ---
Hi TEB's

I've been studying your simple system with the 4H and trend lines combined with trading the 15/30/1H within those trends.  Here's some data on GBPJPY you may find useful.

On a short,

I defined the start of the trend line where the 4H crossed the 80 down....if the down trend started before them I started the trend lines there.  You'll find much of the time this is the start of the trend anyways.  If price broke the trendline and the 4H stock was headed up above 20 I classified that as the trend ended.

I then started trading in the direction of the 4H on the 15M, 30M and 1H independently.

Trades were entered each time the stochastic crossed the 80 down, 61.8 down and 50 down.

There were 2x as many 30 min trades as hourly and 2x as many 15M trades as 30 mins.  Funny how that worked out so nicely.

There is a noticeable breakdown prior to the trend reversing...more on this further below.

Here are the percentages I measured for combined TF trades:

from 80 to 20  94% success  6% failure   50% of trades

from 61.8 to 25 91% success  7% failure   86% of trades

from 50 to 25   92% success  8% failure  100% of trades

25 seemed to be the better level for trades starting from 61.8 and 50...about a 5% difference in increased failures moving the target to 20.

Failure only means the stochastic did not fall to the level on a trade, it does not mean pips lost.  Successes does not always mean a pip gain.  However, for the most part pips losses were small and would have little impact over net gain.

Now, noticing a price break in trend and the 4H stochastic above 20 moving up would help catch a trend break.  More identifying were tags in the stoch movement of trade failures.  These failures would see a trade from the 80 to 20 or 62 to 25 make little movement.  For example most failures happen when the stoch moved from 62 to 50 and then reversed to initiate another down trade or simply went back to 80.  A move from 80 to 20 seeing a reversal around 40 back to 80 was also a break signal.

In other words failures increased across the time frames as/prior to the trend breaking down.  Otherwise, the successes were very high while the trend was in place with just very "close" failures (failures that almost reached target) appearing rarely.  If you do some observations towards the end of trends you will see this quite easily.

To sum up all that.....

Enter the trade with the 4H trend on a short at 80, 61.8 and ride it to the stoch hits 25-20.  When you start having failures, it is a warning sign to stop trading that trend.  That will get you better than 90% success and a good net of pips.

Might call this one Pip Fishing!  Throw out the net and take in the pips.

out

30min 5.3.3

14.3.3

Hi

If its any help the way you described it in you post is correct.

the penny finally dropped for me only recently , but you have to remember the follwing:

4hr 14,3,3 represents a higher tf than 4hr

4hr 5,3,3 represents the 4hr tf

30 mn 14,3,3 represents a higher tf than 30mn(maybe 1hr)

30 mn 5,3,3  reresents 30mn stoch

S0oooo....

If they all correspond simultaneously, then you have FOUR timeframes telling you which direction price is heading.

it is extremely important that you wait( painfull i know!!) for all stoch moves to establish themselves i.e just below 80 or above 20 and that you wait for the relevant candle too close, to confirm position.

today has been the first day i have operated the method with my new understanding of it and the results are soooo much better.keep in mind how relatively quiet its been today..........

Hiya Bago,

Vantage Point is a "Predicting Software", it should be used the other way round. You get the signals from VP and before entering a trade you get your confirmations from TEB's system. Today was a good day for my VP demo account (still testing to make sure I have everything set up the properway).

If you're interested you could check this site out:

http://www.traderchat.com/

It's a site dedicated to VP and has many strategies and reviews there for you to look at. I am sure I am allowed to post this link as it is not in competition with FF.

--- 帖子 #1457 ---
Hi traders,

Some of the members requested some changes to the StochCrossOver indicator.

With this one you can handle to 9 time frames and customize each time frame as you like, or you can just shut it off.

Per time frame you can choose a stoch signal crossover or a overbought/oversold crossover. The parameters for overbought/oversold can also be changed.

You can choose alerts that are combined.

Per time frame you can change the colors, the line widths and styles, etc.

You can even use the same time frames with different alerting.

Regards,

fewhills

--- 帖子 #1459 ---
Hi Tsidki,

I think I understand your problem.

If lines are NOT solid, you can not change the width. So, all none-solid lines only can have 1 as width in MQL4.

Regards,

fewhills

--- 帖子 #1494 ---
hey teb, how do you get your stoch comparisons between the 4hr and the 1hr? In other words, how do you know that the 14.3.3 on the 1hr is similar to the 4hr 5.3.3? Is it just eyeballing it or do you actually calculate it out?

thanks.

--- 帖子 #1495 ---
Stochs are just SMA - but they give you more info ie. over buy/sold

a 15.3.3 on the 3 hour is about the same as a 5.3.3  on the 1 hour

(its a little stronger)

go to your chart and put 3 SMA & a 5 SMA

& they will cross where the stochs do (5.3.3 low/high)

So a 14.3.3 on the 4 hour is a strong 5.3.3 on the 1 hour

TEB

TEB

Hi there thom

NFA has been coming down pretty hard on the forex industry lately.  They have shut down 4 brokers so far this month, due to fraud and/or lack of funding, and they are just warming up.

As far as I know, and I may be wrong, but the names of the brokers that were shut down in June are the following:

FX Option Inc.

Spot FX Clearing Corporation

Trend Commodities Limited

United Global Markets

You can search them on google to find the website address.  Again, if I am wrong about any of these firms, I apologize.

I've been receiving information from some reliable sources, but it's not confirmed yet, but it seems like NFA will shut down any broker that has less than $5 million in funds.  I am not sure of the exact time frame, but it seems like in the next month or two.  That's not the real problem.  The real problem is that I believe some of these bucketshops are not well managed, and when the time comes that they have to go out of business and give all the money back to their clients, they may not have enough.  Or even if they do, it's entirely possible that some of their CEOs may run away with the funds offshore.  So I suggest that you check on your broker's financial capability by going to this link.
http://www.cftc.gov/files/tm/fcm/tmfcmdata0704.pdf

Don't get me wrong, I do believe that some serious firms that currently don't have enough funds could get enough funds to meet the requirements, but I do think that your safety of funds in some smaller firms could be under risk.

The rumor on the street that NFA will raise capital requirement to 9 million by end of this year, but it's still a rumor.  If that happens, I am sure we'll have most small forex brokers go out of business, and we'll probably only have 15 or 20 left, which I think is a good thing.

Anyway, check your broker through the link above, and if you feel you could be at risk, perhaps consider taking your money, before it's too late, and the avalanche starts.

I think this is a very important heads up, and I want to make sure that my subscribers like you are taken cared of before everyone else, so don't post this on any forums, until your own funds are secure...

Thanks

-Felix Homogratus (www.forexbastards.com)

and both stoch on the month are up

over the 80% line down

again I would look to the day which I know is up

read the 14.3.3 1st as trend

then use the 5.3.3 as a trigger

you always need 3 things to go in to a trade that agree

3 stochs or 2 stochs & something else '

I would never sell here unless it breaks that S

they can act as S too ( I don't like PP or Fibbs very much.... just me)

--- 帖子 #1648 ---
I have been asked a few times if you can trade daily

sure get a good day channel (or 4 hour still) this is the key

use a lot of pairs - you will trade less & hold longer

use - month - week- & day charts

(might still keep an eye on the 4 hour)

you will need big SL & TP say 100 pips

but it is in fact easier to trade the higher time frame you do

use the channel for the SL (add 10 pips beyond)

& TP targets when you can

***One last thing find a brooker that close thier day

(books) at a time that works for you.

ie. if you live in N.Y. find one thar close thier books at 5pm est

you just have to have a time you can look at the same everyday!

When is not that important

-get one you trust!!!!!!!!! & size matters  you want NO dealing desk

... you can use one for signs (get a MT4)

& one you use as a bank, ie oanda!!

TEB

but the big thing is I have moved from tool based

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Cable 4 hour

Sure

arrows are touches

yellow area is where we have a good channel formed

in an uptrend
the bottom of the channel is the important line

if it breaks you want out

if the top breaks its proffits

so you want at least 3 touchs on it - tails or bodies

and atleast 2 on the top (3 are better of coarse)

in a down trend the opp. is true

TEB

--- 帖子 #1780 ---
Hi TEB,

I have opened a demo account with Oanda and think it is too good to be true. I am using my brokers real account and Oanda is 10 times better.

Now the question is does Oanda take the spread at the moment of me making a trade? Because I cannot see them taking any spread, as if I had no costs with openning a position? Please clarify.

Regards

Mike

--- 帖子 #1781 ---
Oanda doesn’t charge a commission, so you can't actually see any charges on the statements. But, if you look on the price column on the left side of the platform you will see the sell price and the buy price, the deference is your spread.

Example: If you were to open and close an order without the price moving, you would buy at 1.3600 and sell at 1.35988. It would have cost you 1.2 pips(the spread) for the transaction.

Cheers

oo7_ts

Hey mike o.,

currently I am testing out a hybrid TEB2 using the daily and 1hr and I am entering on the  daily & 1hr 5,3,3 crosses. I will also look for the 14,3,3 for confirmation because when they both line up that can be nice!

I have found that when the 5,3,3 and the 14,3,3 line up you potentially can get some big moves so I use the 14,3,3 as sort of an extra confirmation at times and also I am testing it as an indicator for staying in a trade or not. For example, if I take a trade, I will watch the 14,3,3 blue line (slow stoch) to see if that heads into an overbought or oversold area. when it starts to leave that area, I might get out of a trade. this is something I believe TEB said you can try and I think spudfyre mentions it. however, I am just testing that exit technique.

My results right now are win some lose some. I am trying to get to know the system better and to only take the best setups. My problem is sometimes I do not know when the trade is going against me and thus I stay in too long and get burnt. The system has provided some excellent trades though so I am trying to just stick with it because I can see that it has very good potential. To me I think forex is all about choosing a system that you can relate too and try and learn everything about that system. its strengths and weaknesses. The better I get at knowing a system and cutting my losses, the better my results will be. I really like this system. it is so simple to use and makes so much sense to me. let me know how it is going with you mike o. take care!

On the daily chart cad went oversold on 4/9 or so, and stayed in oversold territory for an entire month -- and during this period fell another 450 pips. Then it took a brief turn up over 20 and shot right back down into "oversold" for an entire month again, until 6/9 or so, to the tune of anoter 500 pips.  That's why stochs (on a single TF especially) are pretty useless during a trending market. Better for ranging, when the oscillator can do what it does best--oscillate. :-D

--- 帖子 #1832 ---
Teb, great job with your trendlines.

It looks to me that the problem you mention here is because you may be looking for a trendline that does not yet exist.  You have some very well defined ones there, but it seems that you made your second 4-hr line where price was at the moment, instead of waiting for a move away from that area first.  In other words, I can make a trendline from any old swing high/low to where price is now, but it doesn't mean that price has actually tested that area yet and moved away from it, creating a boundary.  And while two points may make an acceptable trendline, really 3 or more makes it a much more reliable boundary.

--- 帖子 #1833 ---
Exactly, this has been confusing me for some time.

--- 帖子 #1844 ---
Hey nondisclosure...TEB's statement already contains the answer you are looking for.

If you are using TEB1. Then you would use 5,3,3 stoch settings on the daily, the 1hr and then the 30m chart and wait for all of them to line up (cross).

if you are using TEB2. you would place a 5,3,3 and a 14,3,3 on a 4hr and 30m chart. you would wait for the 4hr stochs to cross then enter on a 30m cross of the stochs.

You can tweak certain timeframes while using this system however dont make them too close. for example looking for a 30m and then a 15m cross. Currently I am using a daily cross then looking for 1hr crosses for entry.

hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #1851 ---
Hey guess121, the stochs, like most if not all indicators, lag behind price action. When price moves, so do the stochs. A stoch cross might be occuring at one point but if price shoots up/down in the opposite direction to the cross, then potentially the stoch can become uncrossed (depending on how high price moves and when it closes).

hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #1857 ---
Hey guess121, backtesting can be successful because you wait for the cross to be solidified ie. wait for the candle to close. When a candle is being formed, the stochs can cross and then uncross depending on how the market is moving. therefore, I will wait for a cross to be confirmed BEFORE placing a trade. In backtesting it should prove to be the same as forward testing as you are waiting for the crosses before making a trade.

--- 帖子 #1858 ---
The TEB EA is based solely on TEB2.  It opens positions based on those orders.

There is no exit strategy in this EA!  But if someone's got some good ideas, I'll entertain them.  right now, it just moves the SL in accordance to the TS values, waits until the SL get hits, then closes order.

Here's the meaning of some of the variables:
MoneyManagement - Change to false to shutdown money management controls.
TradeSizePercent - Change to whatever percent of equity you wish to risk.
Lots - Used only if MoneyManagement if set to false.
LotSize - Contract size of a single lot
Leverage - leverage you get from your brokder
StopLoss - Stop Loss
UseTrailingStop - Use Trailing Stop
TrailingStopType - Type 1 moves stop immediately, Type 2 waits til value of TS is reached
TrailingStop - Pip value of trailing stop
UseTakeProfit - Use Take Profit
TakeProfit - Pip value of where you want take profit taken
Slippage - For definition of slippage, google it.
time1 - Lower time frame.  ie.  using 4h and 30 min, this would be 30
time2 - Higher time frame.  ie.  using 4h and 30 min, this would be 240

Take a look.  Test run, etc.  If we can fine tune it, I would like that.  I'll post all versions as I get input back.  And when we come up w/ something that's final, it'll be here for all to use.

I don't want to mess w/ the MoneyManagement stuff.  I know that works on other EA's I've messed with.

What I want us to work on is Exits and Entrys (Entrys if needed).

--- 帖子 #1874 ---
A more generic, programmable exit:

Close trade when the 14,3,3 stoch. of  1/8th the time period of the long time period to enter the trade gives an opposite signal.

So if 60/240 is used to enter 1/8 of 240 is 30min (14,3,3) is used to exit.

--- 帖子 #1879 ---
So everyone want's a signal generated and NOT a trade opened. Right?

I only had one exit idea posted (http://www.forexfactory.com/showpost...postcount=1878 )

What I'll do is put in the ability to choose your exit timeframe. But the stoch for the exit time frame (exittimeframe in the EA) will be 14,3,3.

New variables:
audioAlert = false; if true it plays annoying sound and flip open dialog box
emailAlert = false; if true it will send an e-mail alert to the e-mail address that's in Metatrader 4 options area.
submitautoorder = false; if true, will submit order for you
closeautoorder = false; if true, will auto close order for you.
exittimeframe = 240; time frame for closeautoorder.

ALL ARE SET TO FALSE BY DEFAULT! In other words, it will not do anything until you set something to true.

Test and play.

Ps. you guys doing back testing (hopefully a full calendar year like 2006) post some results (you get them from the report tab in the strategy tester area in MT4). Of course, if your back testing w/ all the automatic stuff turned on.

Hey TEB, chime in any time buddy!

no, but if you turn moneymanagement off (false), then whatever lot number you put in will be used per trade.

--- 帖子 #1887 ---
Now I remember why I didn't use this in trend trading.  The EA resets itself each time a new candle is formed.

Kills the whole thing.  It'll work for Dustin when he's doing news due to the volitility of it, but not when your trading trends.

IF you were to use this trading trends, you should use it on a daily chart.  That way settings won't be reset on a new candle.

--- 帖子 #1891 ---
Actually it did.  Your chart is the 30 min I assume.

You drew your line in the wrong spot.

One candle behind your big blue line would be where the order was actually opened.  If you change the time on your chart to 4 hour, you'll see that it entered at the right spot on 4 hour.

Remember, the candle BEFORE the arrow is the one that makes the determination on wether to open the order.

--- 帖子 #2009 ---
TEB3 SIMPLE

1. Remove everything from your charts ....I mean everything!!

2. Add two sma 4 closed (Blue) sma 5 open (red)

(if you don't have open & closed then 3 &7 SMA works also)

3. move to the weekly chart get trend (blue & red lines )

4. move to the daily charts to get triggers ( pink arrows)

5. move to the 4 hour to get comformation ( black arrows)

3rd charts

week charts-  you see trend blue & red lines only go with them

day charts - are triggers ( pink arrows) & stops (Pink "X")

4 hour - conformations of buy/sell (black arrows)

you want all 3 going the same ways

you are in and out on the day charts.

when the weekly turns you are out big time

you can take 1/2 when the 4 hour turns

or add to your trade when the 4 hour goes the way you want

SL atlease 50pips

TP let it ride.

you will have small loses - & big wins

its that simple.

TEB,

I am most greatful for everything you have shared. It has taken 5 days to read every post to this point. I might have been faster had I not been playing with each of the systems you have presented here. A sincere thanks to everyone else participating here as well.

It is very interesting that I have stumbled upon quite a few pips in the last few days. I'm starting to look like some kind of genius trader  . But of course my genius is only my ability to synthesize what is put before me. I certainly haven't created anything to date. However, I am having some fun looking at a merge of some of your systems with some old tools I have developed or been working with. Rest assured if I find something with some strong correlation I will not hesitate to share it with the rest of you.

Thanks again. And a special thanks to you coders out there who are swinging away at this. I beleive TEB is not keen on the automation, and I certainly understand. But until I have more money and time to sit at the screen and run this more like a full time business, I'm looking for every advantage I can to find entries and apply exit strategy updates when I'm away at my day job. I am learning to code myself and everything you folks present is real grist for my mill.

To that end, let me suggest that a complete EA is not always what we might be looking for. Some code that allows you to say, identify a trendline already placed on your chart with an offset, for a stop loss. Or maybe an EA that can recognize two lines as a channel for a stop loss and TP for an existing position... Of course we'd have to put a trade on with a magic number or provide an active (open) order number to make it work... and some object identifiers for the lines. At least that way you could manage a position with an EA while you had to be away. If you come back, and the position is still open you just turn off the EA and manage it on your own. Working in this way would lead you toward automating a full EA that recognizes channels you personally draw. Then all you have to do is add a component that recognizes the channels -- that's the easy part, right?  . But really, building a tool that applies rules for SL and TP on an existing position using channels we identify to it would allow me to keep a position open with a known self adjusting risk:reward while I'm away at work. I think most people would prefer that to closing a winning position or placing a stop loss, and it would allow you programmers to progress toward something more fully automated anyway.

That's much more than I intended to post. Sorry to those it bothers... I know you are out there. But I really appreciate what everyone has contributed. Thanks so very much.

Qman

--- 帖子 #2057 ---
The channel format is a part of a template that was originally developed for Orange Roshnan's SRDCII system (check the thread, lots of good stuff there). Much of the method is about channels and price movements in the channels.

The channel I've used is a Fib channel, and when the template is activated, the additional lines are automatically drawn in the channel.

You can use additional lines (or the four quartals) for openings. FOr instance, don't open a buy position if the price in topmost quartal during uptrend, even if other indicators like stochs would propose that. Or, whenever the lowest quartal is entered during uptrend, open a buy position.

Lines can also be used for exits, e.g. close half of your position when the middle line is crossed, and let the rest run.

The SRDCII method description contains a collection of rules that can be applied with the template.

R

|

--- 帖子 #2063 ---
The message probably came out a bit too harsh. We need to keep in mind that TEB3 is a winning system, which requires only a small amount of effort to be run. Unlike many other systems presented in this forum, it is also explicit, and the results are repeatable. Applied to four main pairs, it is likely to give some 300-400 pips per month. Not bad at all...

I'm personally more fond of TEB2. When it is combined with channels (which can overcome TEB2 difficulties during strong, longlasting trends) the  results can be really good. Channels (or trendlines), when properly used, is imo the only indicator that is capable of really forecasting future price development. All the others are more or less documenting what has happened, ie what the price did.

The problem with channels is that they are subjective, and difficult to determine when trend is chaning. I'm still developing TEB2-channel rule set for my purposes.

I use 4H and 30m. Also sometimes I see at the daily but my main tool is the 4H and the trigger is the 30m.

It is exactly as TEB said. There are times when you can cheat a bit (i.e. when not both stochs cross on the 30m) and still make money but if someone follows the rules it is good as it gets ( I said that yesterday but i truly believe it and I trade the FX for a bit over 2 years now).

In addition, spend some time (5-10 mins) before you start trading and try to spot the 4H channels. Every day there will be definetely 2-3 pairs that form decent 4H channels (by decent I mean at least 2 tops and 2 bottoms). When you find them, use them. It is almost a crime for somebody not to use the 4H channels when spotted.

--- 帖子 #2107 ---
I looked at TEB 1 when it was posted but didn't progress with it. I recently came across TEB 3 and a quick inspection has sparked an huge interest in its possibilities.

Can someone familiar/experienced (TEB63 ?) with this method confirm a few details please?

The chart indicators are simply: a SMA 4 Close (blue) and a SMA 5 Open(red).

CHart 1 (weekly)

An MA cross here gives the trend direction.

Q Does this trend remain valid ('hold') until the opposite cross?

Q When the MA slopes deteriorate does this also indicate the end of the trend?

CH2 (daily)

This chart is where trading is done. A cross of the MAs in the same direction as the trend on CH1 indicates a possible entry (pink arrow).

Q Exit is indicated by a reverse cross? (pink 'X')

CH3 (4 hour)

Is used for confirmation. An MA cross here in the same direction confirms the entry seen on CH2.

Q Should the confirmation cross occur AFTER the entry cross on CH2 or does it not matter?

Additions and 50% TPs are possible at new H4 crosses or turns -Q as long as the CH2 trend continues?

My initial tests on various charts shows big possibilities for TEB 3. Most of the pairs I've looked at seem to work very well but does anyone have any recommendations which pairs to use?

R

--- 帖子 #2126 ---
Guys, how do you actually use channels?

Here is one way I use channel info. The channel here is pointing up, and it sometimes happens that stochs on 4H chart do not show when the trend (here downtrend - the thick red line) changes. For instance in this example you could not draw the last thick green line using 4H stochs, they both stay well above 20, and you would miss the next upmove.

So, I check the 1H chart and if both stochs on that chart visit under 20 like here, I take that as a signal that the trend is up, and start opening buy positions based on 30M chart. Especially, if the price is near channel borders. In this way I ease up the TEB2 rules a little, depending on the channel direction.

Note that this 1H stoch lows near the earlier down channel upper boundary also indicates the end for this channel.

R

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Personally i trade the TEB2

to answer your questions: It is better for the lines to cross the overbought/oversold areas when they cross, this is a strong signal.

It is even stronger if all of the crosses happen approximately the same time (4H and 30m).

However I still trade (observing 4H channels and candles) if the crosses do not take place in the overbought/sold territories and it is still profitable.

Hope it helps

the difference is that you do not have always to wait for the 4h to close and then move to 30m.

Another thing i want to add. There are times that the 4H is crossed up and the 30m is crossed down. when the 30 crosses up again and the 4h is the same it is still a very good signal.+

Also this method applies much better to the European session and the overlapping of European and US session. especially now that yen crosses are affected by the DOW and NASDAQ

Hope it helps

--- 帖子 #2216 ---
Hi there,

TEB might have additional comments to this, but imo the idea is to identify the long term trend using a slower timeframe (like a 4H chart where you insert a thick green or red line as the trend on that TF changes), and then move to faster TF (1H) and pick up there the spots where the trend changes to the direction of the slower TF. In this way we make sure that we are trading with the trend, not against it, trying to minimize risk and maximising the profit.

So, if on 4H TF the trend is down, you place sell positions, when the stochs on 1H have been over 80 and fall again below that limit. If you get in too early, like in the example you show, there is a high risk that the price still continues to move against you, as stochs have not reached the desired (overbought) value.

R
